% This file is based on the new high-resolution Berkeley Earth global temperature
% data set.  It expands upon the previous Berkeley Earth temperature data set by
% including predictive structures based on historical weather patterns.  While,

% development and substantial revisions remain possible if significant issues
% are identified.

% This file contains an ensemble summary of land surface average temperature
% temperature estimated from the new high-resolution Berkeley Earth
% land-surface temperature fields

%

%

% This file provides an ensemble of alternative reconstructions of land surface 
% temperature that are meant to sample the full set of uncertainties underpinning
% this temperature analysis.
